create table Trainer
(
    email        varchar(320)              not null
        primary key,
    password     char(60)                  not null,
    fullname     varchar(200) charset utf8 null,
    address      varchar(200) charset utf8 null,
    phone        char(11)                  null,
    gender       varchar(20)               null,
    status       int                       not null,
    profileImage varchar(2000)             null,
    dob          bigint                    null,
    yearOfExp    float                     null,
    rating       float                     null,
    deviceID     varchar(1000)             null
);

create index status
    on Trainer (status);
